puis oevre la taille as oncines, et depart bellement l’artere des toiles, tant qu’ele soit descoverte;	Then make a cut with a lancet, and carefully separate the artery from the tissues, until it is exposed.
puis boute desoz li une aguille, et la fai percier jusc’a l’autre costeit, et estraint l’artere d’un fil double en II leus, selonc ceu que je t’ai ensigniet en l’estraction des II arteres qui sont en temples;	Then place a needle beneath it, and pierce it all the way to the other side, and tie the artery with a double thread in two places, according to what I have taught you in the extraction of the two arteries in the temples.
puis point le leu qui est entre les II liens d’un intromissoire tant que li sans en isse qui i est, et soit deliiez li aposteme;	Then prick the place between the two ties with a probe until the blood that is in it comes out, and the abscess be released.
puis amenistre la cure que enjanre bowe, tant que li liien chient;	Then apply the cure that promotes suppuration, until the tie falls off.
puis cure ceu d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then cure it with a suitable ointment, until it is healed.
et se li apostemes est por la taille de la voinne, si covient que tu teignes a ta main ceu que tu pues de l’aposteme a tout le cuir, puis boute l’aguille desoz le leu que tu tiens a ta main, et la fai percier, et i ait I fil double, si que tu le trais de l’autre costeit;	And if the abscess is near the vein's incision, you should hold what you can of the abscess with your hand, then place the needle underneath where you are holding, and pierce it, and use one double thread, and pull it from the other side.
puis lie l’aposteme, si com je t’ai dit, ou liien de l’une de II pars as II chiés dou fil;	Then tie the abscess, as I told you, or tie one of the two ends of the thread to the two ends.
et se tu doutes que li filz n’isse fuer, si i reboute une autre aguille a tout I fil desoz tout l’aposteme a l’incision de la premiere aguille, et estraint les filz en IIII leus;	And if you doubt that the thread won't stay, then insert another needle through the thread underneath the entire abscess, at the incision of the first needle, and tighten the threads in four places.
puis cope l’aposteme tant que li superfluitez en isse, puis cope la superfluiteit dou keur et laisse ceu qui est liiez;	Then cut the abscess until the excess comes out, then cut the excess from the core and leave what is tied.
puis met sus I drapeil moilliet en vin et en oile, puis li amenistre cures de tentes et d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then place a damp cloth in wine and oil, and then administer cures of poultices and ointments until it is healed.
des apostemes des ners	Of abscesses of the nerves
Ausi com aposteme vienent en l’artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.	Just as abscesses come to the artery and vein, abscesses come to the nerves when they are struck, or through excessive labor, and similar things.
Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c’est I grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor;	And this happens more often to the shoulders and hands and in all places where there are joints, and it is a grievous abscess, and its color resembles the color of the body, and is in many dispositions without pain;
et quant on l’estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n’est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur;	and when it is squeezed tightly, the patient feels pain, and it is not deep within the body, but beneath the heart;
et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer:	and moves well in all directions, and does not go forward or backward, or below or above, and that which is in the joints should not be cut with iron:
par aventure i vanroit contraction;	perhaps contraction would result;
et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.	and that which is on the head or forehead, split the skin with a spatula.
Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine;	If the abscess is small, hold it with tweezers and cut it at its root;
et s’il est grans, si le sospent a l’oncine, et l’escorche, puis l’oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if it is large, suspend it with forceps, and scrape it, then remove it and stitch the wound together, and treat it until it is healed.
des grosses boces pendans	of large hanging boils
Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d’aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros;	Sometimes it occurs in the belly and nowhere else, a disease called "fungus" because of its resemblance to mushrooms, and the root is subtle, and the head large;
et en i a de petis et de mout grans;	and some are small and some very large;
et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.	and I saw a man who had two in his belly that were more like fungi than anything else, and there was no difference, and they were white, and had fine roots, and were slightly split, and moisture often ran from them.
Je les copai et trovai en l’un XVIII onces pesant, et en l’autre VI З., et li ovraiges en l’incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l’artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine;	I cut them and found eighteen ounces in one, and six in the other, and the work in the incision is such that you look to see if the patient is moist, and the color of the fungus is white and moist and of subtle roots;
si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.	if the cut is wide, and the cautery iron is present.
Car au taillier vient maintes fois trop grans decorremens de sanc, et se li sans te vaint, si te haste donques dou cauterizer;	For in the cutting, there are often excessive flows of blood, and if the blood overwhelms you, then hasten to cauterize;
et se tu vois le malaide espoanteit et paourous de l’incision dou fer, si prent I fil de plonc bien fait, et en lie l’artelul si com nos avons dit, et le laisse II jors;	and if you see the patient terrified and fearful of the incision of the iron, then take a well-made lead thread, and bind the fungus to it as we have said, and leave it for two days;
et puis le restraint, et ne cesser d’estraindre lou fil de plonc tant qu’il cope l’artelul, et chiece par lui sens travail;	and then restrain it, and do not cease to restrain the lead thread until it cuts the fungus and falls off effortlessly.
et se les racines sont grosses, si a paour au coper meismement por le ventre, mais tu em pues bien coper la moitiet, puis le cauterize qu’il ne reviegne;	and if the roots are large, there is fear in cutting, especially toward the belly, but you may well cut half of it, then cauterize it so it does not return;
puis cure la plaie, et garde que tu ne coper le thelul qui est de fuxe color et de povre sens et de lait regart.	then treat the wound, and be careful that you do not cut the pellicle which is of a fixed color and of poor sensation and milky appearance.
Car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, et je venrai a la cure de chancre ci aprés.	For it is a festering abscess, and I will come to the treatment of ulcers later.
quant li boude ist fuer	when the boil is mature
Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit;	If the appearance of the boil comes from a cauterized wound or a split surface, and is on the belly, and some boils arise, as happens in other ruptures, or from blood flowing from veins or arteries according to what is stated above, or from wind;
et se c’est par la routure dou syfac et par l’issue dou bouel, si est li color de l’aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.	and if it is from a split surface and the boil's emergence, the color of the abscess resembles the body's color, and is a slight thing without pain, and appears with diverse emergence.
Et se c’est por l’issue de l’intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l’entree dou bain et por fort travail.	And if it is because of the emergence of the intestine, then it is more diverse, and when one presses it with their fingers, it will recede and then return, and perhaps it is hard, and grows greatly at the entrance of the bath and from hard labor.
Et se c’est por moistor, c’est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie;	And if it is due to moisture, it is a slight thing, and appears well when you press it with your hand, and does not constrain it at all;
et se c’est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit;	and if it is due to blood, the abscess appears large and hard by these signs, and is fixed according to a quantity;
et se c’est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l’artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.	and if it is due to wind, it is soft to the touch, and the work is that you look to see if the appearance is due to the blood of the artery, or the vein, or wind.
Si covient que tu laisses la cure.	Then you should abandon the treatment.
Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t’ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l’artere et por la voine.	For there is doubt and fear, as I have told you in the chapter on abscesses, for the artery and for the vein.
Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude;	And if the appearance is due to the intestine or the bowels, you should instruct the patient to hold his breath and lie straight, then mark all around the area;
puis le comande a gesir sovin entre tes mains, puis va entor le leu que tu as signiet a tout le spatumile, puis estent la moitiet de l’aposteme au desus a tout le grant uncine;	then instruct him to lie often between your hands, then go around the area you marked with all the spatulas, then extend half of the abscess upward with the entire large forceps;
puis le lie entor d’un fil fort, ou d’une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz;	then bind it around with strong thread, or a strong silk cord tightly, and let the wound be free from the bandage;
puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine;	then open the extended half of the abscess above the bandage, and put your index finger in, and search for the intestine;
se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre;	if you find it caught by the bandage, untie it, and push the intestine outside the belly;
et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit;	and if you find the bowel, take it with the forceps, and cut off the excess;
et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier;	and if the artery or vein opposes you, go around carefully, then return to your work and take two needles, and put two strong threads in them, and put the two needles around what you have done in a cross-shape so that you make it pierce;
puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi;	then tighten the abscess in four places over the needles, and if you wish, remove the needles, and leave the place until it rots, and the dead flesh will fall away by itself;
ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit;	or you cut it when it is softened and rotten, then treat it as necessary, and heal the abscess as we have said;
et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu’il couvient, et soude le leu.	and draw out the blood or moisture that you find, then treat the place as necessary, and close the wound.
dou chancre	about chancre
Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer;	We have discussed the types of chancre, and how one should treat them with medicine, and how to avoid using iron for treatment;
et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement;	and we say that chancre develops in the breast, and great care is needed in its treatment, and the ancients said that when a chancre is in a place where it can be scraped off, like a chancre on the nipples and in the thigh, and similar places, it should be completely removed when it is in the early stages;
et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner;	and when it is large and old, you should not approach it, for I have never been able to cure any such.
ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.	No one has ever cured one before me.
Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire;	And the treatment, when it is in a place where it can be removed, as we have said, is that you purge the patient of black bile on occasion;
puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide I boin leu por faire l’ovraige;	then bleed him if there is obvious fullness, then prepare the patient in a good place to do the treatment;
puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier;	then throw away your lancets or cauteries, and the scab from all sides, and remove it from all sides without leaving anything;
et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	and let the blood flow freely, and wipe the place well with your hand or some object, and if the bleeding makes you oppose the incision of the artery or vein, cauterize it until the blood is stopped;
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it with another treatment until it is healed.
de ydropisie	of dropsy
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer:	We have already discussed the various types of dropsy, how water collects, the signs of each type, and the treatment using medicine and iron:
si est eclites soulement;	if only it is eclipsis.
et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances:	and one should not use iron in these two types:
c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose;	that is to say, tympanites and yposarche, for it is a deadly thing;
donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses;	Therefore, when treating this type of dropsy called "eclites" with medicine, and the treatment is ineffective, check if the patient is weak, or if they have another illness besides dropsy, such as a bowel issue or similar problems;
si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance;	if you should not touch it with iron, for there is danger;
et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:	and if you see a patient of strong constitution, and they have no illness other than dropsy alone, and they are neither too young nor too old, you should proceed as follows:
lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	Raise the patient upright in your hands, and the attendant should press on the belly, forcing the water to the lowest part of the chest, then take the spine-shaped spatula according to this form:
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	And let it be sharp on both sides.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;	pointed, and yet not so deep that it can reach the intestines when inserted, and cannot cause injury;
puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines:	then see if the dropsy is lodged towards the intestines:
si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil;	if so, you should cut into the cavity, three straight cuts below the knife;
et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois;	and if the dropsy is due to a liver ailment, let your cut be on the left side of the cavity, three cuts;
et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;	and if it is due to the spleen, let it be on the right, and it is not appropriate for the patient to lie on the cut so that the superfluities do not flow to that weak spot;
puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor;	then pierce all the skin with the instrument, and apply it, and lift your hand through all the space between the skin and the surface, just as in skinning, to the amount of a fingernail or even more;
puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	then pierce the surface until the space reaches the empty spot, and that is the place of the water, then draw it out, and apply this instrument, of which this is the shape:
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus;	And it is similar to a chain of fine silver, and is of bronze or light bronze, and has a small hole at the bottom part;
et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus;	and on one side there are three holes;
et II d’autre part, et I d’autre;	and two on the other side, and one on the other;
et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	and the head is cut like a feather, and this is the shape of the incision with which the scribes cut the feather:
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument;	at the top is the nozzle, so that when the instrument comes to the water, it immediately descends upon the instrument;
vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;	empty then one-half or one-third, for if you empty more than is fitting at that moment, perhaps the patient will die from the resolution of his spirit from the wound, or he will collapse, or he will approach death;
mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz;	but empty according to the quantity of its virtue, and according to what the dispositions of the patient's virtue signify, and his pulses;
puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere;	then withdraw the instrument and retain the water, and it is now retained due to the heart that stops the hole that is on the surface, of which I have spoken, that you pierce in this manner;
puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;	then repeat the instrument the next day, if you see the patient suffering this, and draw a small quantity of water;
fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	do this for some days, and be careful not to overdo it so that only a little water remains.
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre;	And if you doubt about the patient, and you leave too much water, then cure him with a hot grave or hot sand, and through much sweating or baths and the sun, and have him drink;
et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	and cure him with drying medicines until he is healthy, and cauterize on the stomach and on the liver and on the spleen after the water extraction, as I said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	of the blockage of the penis
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	Sometimes children are born who have no opening in the penis, or the opening is small, or it is not in its proper place.
Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout I spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme:	If it is necessary, quickly pierce it with a very thin needle according to this shape:
puis met ou pertus I clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi III jors ou IIII et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet;	then place a thin lead plug in the opening, and bind it and keep it like this for three or four days.  When he wants to urinate, remove the plug, and let him urinate, and then replace it;
et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	and perhaps it is not necessary, for the urine that comes to flow will not leave it closed.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera.	Those whose opening is small, are treated with a lead plug, as we have said, and it will enlarge.
Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut;	Those whose opening is not in its place are wounded, for some are born with the opening at the head of the penis, so that they cannot urinate before raising their penis;
et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	and they cannot conceive because the matter cannot reach the womb, and that is a bad illness.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient;	And the manner of the work is that the patient lies often on their back, then extends the head of the penis and cuts it as if the size of a feather, so that the opening falls into the middle, as is appropriate;
et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	and beware of the bleeding that often occurs, and if it happens, stop it with what stops blood, and heal the wound until it is healthy.
des pustules de la verge	of the sores on the penis
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide;	Many times these sores appear on the penis, and it is an unsightly appearance of flesh;
et en i a malignes et non malignes;	and some are malignant and some are not;
si covient que tu les preignes a I oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien;	so you must take them with a fine forceps, and cut and clean them all, then put moistened cotton on Egyptian ointment;
puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat with Diafinicon ointment until they are healed.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.	And if the sore is malignant, of foul color and stinking, you must apply cautery.
Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier;	When you have cut it, and if the ulcer is partly on the shaft and partly under the skin, you must first remove the part of the ulcer that is inside.
et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer.	and when it is closed, treat the part on the outside.
Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion;	For when you treat it together, the shaft of the penis is not safely healed, it may be pierced, and blackness and corruption come to the penis and the testicles.
si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	You must remove all that is black and corrupt, then apply a plaster of honey and flour, made from pomegranate bark and herbs, then treat it with other remedies until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:	And if a discharge of blood comes, administer the lunar cautery according to this form:
Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble:	The cautery aids two conditions together:
c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption;	that is to say, to the discharge of blood, and to the corruption;
et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi;	And if the head of the penis is corrupt and retracted, you must place a lead tube or conduit on the penis, and the patient must urinate through it;
et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;	And when the skin is inflamed at the head of the penis, which happens to those who have not been circumcised, or it happens due to a wound or abscess, then you must cauterize it with a sharp instrument, until the adhesion is broken, and the head of the penis is freed from all sides;
et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a I spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil;	And if it is a serious matter to divide it, you should cauterize a small area on the head of the penis and the surrounding skin;
puis dessevre belement entre II, et i met I subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	Then carefully separate them and place a thin, soaked linen cloth over it, to prevent further inflammation.
de la circoncision	Of circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies;	Circumcision is not simply a separation of the continuation like other wounds;
toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	However, when we perform this operation of our own volition, and especially on children, it is necessary that we perform the best and least harmful operation.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not prescribe circumcision for their children, for they do not use it in their law, and we have only what we have acquired through experience.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor I dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule;	For I have seen the greatest part of the masters and noblemen who performed circumcision with a knife, and by force, and with a whole new razor;
si fuioit li keurs car il i a II toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	If the heart fled because there are two blades, and perhaps one above is cut, and the one below remains.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre;	Or it must be cut again, and the pain is doubled, and the cleansing of the instrument does not ensure the tip of the limb;
et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	and with the cleansing of the nail, perhaps the iron slips, and the work is ruined, and many times they are born such that they do not need cleansing, and I have seen it.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	Of the cleansing that is done with force, to the entire thread of the wire, I have found the goodness of the experiment, for the force cuts just as well above as below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens;	For when you press your hand, it cuts equally in one whole instant;
mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir;	but let the wire be well tight around the skin;
et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	and let the manner of the first work be such that you make the child, if he understands, think that you are only tying the thread around the rod, and then you can make him happy in every way you can;
puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens;	then place him between your hands upright, and hold the forces between your hands or under your feet so that the child does not see them, nor any of the instruments;
puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens;	then place your hand on the rod and blow into the heart, and pull it up until the head of the rod is in;
puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien;	then clean it well of the dirt that has gathered there, then tie the marked place with a double thread, then tie it below one stitch to the other stitch;
et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;	and hold it with your two fingers by the second stitch at the thumb and index finger, and cut between the two stitches, then lift the heart quickly and pull the head of the rod;
puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres;	then let the blood flow drop by drop, for that is the remedy;
et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and put powder on and on top of the powder a cloth dipped in a mixture of a boiled egg tempered with rose water, mixed with good fresh rose oil, and leave it on until the next day, and treat it with another treatment until it is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste:	The form of strength for cleansing is this:
li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	the two blades should be taut and sharp, and the blades should also be as large as the handle equally:
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision;	The error in the cleansing is when the heart is inside the incision;
donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;	Then you must extend it to your fingernail, so that the place does not form an abscess;
et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	and cut it evenly, and if you cannot hold it to your fingernail, hold it with pliers, and then cut it.
Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement;	And if three days pass, and that which is beneath the rod is swollen, let it be until the hot abscess is calmed, and lightly scrape it;
si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	cut it as you can, and be careful of the part of the rod, this will not harm it at all.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;	Then cure the place with things suitable for wound powder, as we have said in treating powders, and if one cuts too deeply into the heart, and it goes above, it will not harm.
cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then cure it, as we have said, until it is healed.
dou retenement de l’urine	Concerning the retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	The retention of urine is due to blockage by stone, or congealed blood, or pus, or dead flesh, or similar things, as we have said in the division.
et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;	And if the urine is not released, and you see the retention is due to a stone lodged in the bladder's neck or opening, then the patient should be bent over their knees.
et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet;	And their feet should be placed on their back, and they should extend their abdomen from the upper part of their back, and the patient should contract their abdomen as much as they can.
et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	And then the neck of the bladder is constricted, pushing the stone upwards, so that the urine is released.
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme:	And if it does not come, as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you should apply extraction with an instrument called a "syringe," of which this is the shape:
et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil;	And it should be made of fine, light silver, like the feathers of a bird.
et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	And it should be one and a half palms long, and thin at the head.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue;	And the method of releasing the urine is that you take a double thread, and tie a small piece of wool or cotton to the end, and insert the end of the thread into the syringe.
et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	And cut the excess wool, and push it to the tip of the syringe, then anoint the syringe with oil or butter and egg white, and make the patient sit on a stool, and lubricate the bladder and penis with moist oil and olive oil and warm water.
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude;	Then gently insert the syringe into the penis, until it reaches the root of the penis, then pull the penis upward towards the groin;
puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors;	Then push the syringe forward towards the bladder, and the patient feels it coming up to the empty space, and this is not done correctly unless the channel it goes through is twisted;
puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	Then pull the thread with all the little bit of wool, and the urine follows the wool, then pull it out, and make the urine flow;
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	And repeat the syringe until the bladder is emptied, and the patient is relieved.
des maladies de la vessie	Of the diseases of the bladder
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When burns or blood comes into the bladder, or rot is gathered there, and you wish to instill liquids and medicines, do so using the entire instrument called a "clepsydra," and this is its form:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus:	It is closed, and has three openings:
II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;	Two on one side, and one on the other, as you see;
et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	and the channels through which the medicine flows should be such that they seal well the urethra without additional support, so that one can draw out moisture, and insert it when necessary;
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;	And when you wish to put your medicines into the bladder, place the tip of the instrument into the moisture, and pull on the string inside;
si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;	so you will draw the moisture into the instrument, and then forcefully push the string back inside;
si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	then the moisture will enter inside, and will go to the bladder immediately, so that the patient will feel it;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie:	and this is the form of the subtle enema with which one enemas the bladder:
si est ci:	if it is so:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;	And it is of silver or of arch, and the head is higher;
et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;	and below at the breast where the ligament falls;
puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;	then take a sheep's bladder and put in the moisture with which you wish to enema the bladder, then tie it between the two breasts using a well-made double thread, and heat the moisture a little over the fire;
puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	then put the head of the clyster into the rod, then hold your hand over the bladder, allowing all the moisture to enter, until the patient feels that the moisture has indeed reached the bladder;
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor;	and if you do not have a bladder, then take a piece of parchment, and make a circle of it, and pierce it roundly around;
puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;	then put a strong thread in these holes, then assemble the circle as one would assemble a tile, and put within it what you want of oil and moisture and water, and tie it in the instrument;
et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	and do as you did with the bladder, pressing with your hand until the moisture comes to the bladder.
de la piere	of the stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;	We have already said in the division the kinds of stones, and the extraction together with medicines;
et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	and have spoken of the difference between stones formed in the kidneys, and all the signs, and in which stone one should work with a cutting tool;
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	and in the bladder, and in the penis;
et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	and I will tell you openly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;	I say that the stone formed in the bladder happens more often to children, and this is a sign that the urine leaks from the bladder like water in its subtlety;
et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;	and there appears gravel, and the patient scratches his penis, and it hangs down many times, and then stiffens;
et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;	and from much of this leakage the foundation [of the body] weakens;
et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	and the healing is easy in children until they are four years old, and is very difficult in old men, and is moderate in young people, in those who are between youth and old age;
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	and the cure is easier for those who have large stones than for those who have small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to the cure, it is necessary first to cleanse the patient with a clyster, to remove all the filth which is in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For it sometimes hinders in seeking the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;	Then take the patient by the feet, and lift and move him downwards, so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and sometimes comes out from a high position.
puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;	then make him sit between your hands prepared, and his hands are under his thighs, so that the bladder is completely inclined downwards;
puis la quier et la touche dedens;	then seek and touch it inside;
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	if you feel the stone in the space, then hurry now to cut above the stone.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;	And if it does not fall out upon touching it entirely, then moisten your index finger with oil from your left hand, if the patient is a child, or your middle finger, if the patient is a fully grown young man;
et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;	and put it into its base, and seek the stone, and when you feel it with your finger, then draw it to the neck of the bladder;
puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	then press against your finger, and push it out to the place where you wish to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;	And order the minister to press the bladder with his hand, and order him to stretch his right hand up to the nipples, and with his left hand to remove the skin underneath the nipples in the part where the incision will be made;
puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	then apply the spatula, the shape of which is this:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;	And make an incision between the nipples and the fundament, not in the middle but along the left side;
et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	and it should be straight over the stone, and your fingers should be on the fundament, and the incision should be wide at the outer edge and narrow inside, according to the size of the stone, not too large;
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;	perhaps the pressure from your fingers on the fundament will make it jump out without difficulty;
et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:	and know that there are stones that have angles and edges:
si est griés a issir;	if it is difficult to remove;
et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	and there are some that are smooth, like a ball, and round, whose removal is easy.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;	For those with angles and edges, make the incision larger;
et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;	and if it does not come out, you should use pliers that are like a file at the head, to tightly grasp the stone so that it does not escape;
ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;	or you insert a subtle, curved instrument under it;
et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	and if you cannot thus extract it, widen the opening slightly, and if the blood flows, cauterize it with vitriol;
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	and if there is more than one stone, first remove the largest one from the bladder's neck, then cut, then pull it out forcefully, and remove the smaller ones afterward, if there are any more.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if it is very large, it must be chipped away, and a larger incision made.
Car II choses avienent au malaide:	For two things happen to the patient:
ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;	either he dies, or his urine comes out constantly because the opening cannot heal;
mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	but nevertheless, try to pull it out, or break it with pliers, until you pull it out in pieces;
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;	and when you have completed your work, fill the wound with frankincense, aloe, and dragon's blood, and compress it, and place a damp cloth soaked in oil and wine, or oil and rose water and cold water, over it to soothe the hot abscess;
puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	then bind the patient's neck, and do not loosen the bandage until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you loosen it, wash the area well with oil and water, then treat it with diafinicon and basilicon ointments until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:	And if hot abscesses come to the wound and corrosions, and congealments of blood in the bladder, and be thus retained the urine, which is known in such a way that without interruption with the urine:
boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	Then put your finger into the wound and extract that blood, for if it remains, it will corrode the bladder and rot it;
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then wash the wound with water and herbs and salt, and assist him in every way that you can, until he is healed;
et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	and it is necessary that every time you treat him, that you bind his two thighs together, and gather the medicines on the area.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;	And if the stone is small, and it is in the passage of the penis, and stuck inside, and the urine cannot exit;
si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	if you treat it as I have said before, that you cut it many times, one is excused from the cutting through this treatment.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have already proven it thus.
Pren I foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a III angles fichiees en I tison:	Take an iron implement according to this form and let it have three angles fixed into a single point.
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;	then take a thread and tie it around the penis below the stone, so that it cannot return into the bladder;
puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;	then insert the implement into the penis gently, until it reaches the stone;
et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;	and turn the implement in your hand against the stone little by little, until you can pierce the stone on the other side;
si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	then the urine will come out quickly, then press your hand on that which remains of the stone inside the penis.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	Then it will quickly break, and jump out with the urine, and the patient is cured;
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;	and if you cannot do this for any reason that prevents it, tie a thread under the stone and another above, then cut the penis at the stone between the two threads, then pull it out, and untie the thread, and cleanse the congealed blood that is in the wound;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it until it is healed.
de la piere des femmes	of the stone of women
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	Sometimes a stone is embedded in women, and if this happens, the cure is difficult, and is forbidden for three things:
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	one is that perhaps the woman is a virgin;
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	and the second is that one cannot find a woman knowledgeable enough to reveal herself to healers, especially if she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	And the third way is that perhaps one cannot find a woman knowledgeable in this art of hands;
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	And the fourth way is that the stone in a woman is deeper than in a man, so it requires a deeper incision, and there is great fear.  And if necessity requires this, you must take a skilled healer, and it is difficult to find one. And if you find none, seek a subtle, skilled healer;
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	and present a wise woman experienced in women's health, or a woman who knows part of the art, and instruct her to do what you command regarding the examination of the stone;
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	and look closely if the woman is a virgin:
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	Then she must insert her finger into the opening and search for the stone;
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	And if she finds it, she should hold it under her finger, and she should be instructed to place her finger on the affected area, and press her left hand firmly against the bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	If she finds it, she should move it gradually from the entrance of the bladder downwards, until it reaches the root of the thigh;
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	Then cut into the stone at the root of the thigh, opposite the middle of the opening, where the stone appears to be positioned, and feel for the stone in that area;
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	and do not move her finger over or under the stone, and let the incision be initially small;
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	Then insert the instrument into the incision; if you feel the stone, enlarge the wound until the stone can be forced out, and know that there are many types of stones:
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	that is to say, small and large, rough and smooth, long and round, and those that have ridges.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	So recognize the signs in order to know the outcome.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if the blood overwhelms you, place powdered vitriol on the wound and hold it for an hour until the blood is stopped;
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	then return to your work until the stone is forced out, and have the instruments that I have told you about for the extraction of stones, to help you with your task.
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	And if the blood overwhelms you, and it's from a cut artery, place the powder on the wound and bind it with cloths and bandages, and do not continue this, and leave the stone and do not remove it, lest the patient should die.
puis cure la plaie.	Then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood has subsided, and the wound is healed, then return to your work, until the stone is forced out.
de hernie carnouse	of fleshy hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	Watery hernia is nothing other than an accumulation of moisture or white pus, beneath the curvature of the testicles, which contains the testicle;
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	and is called "pus", and sometimes is properly in the tissue of the testicle, so that one might think it is another testicle;
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	and it is the skin of the testicle between the white pus that we have mentioned;
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	and this happens rarely.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the generation of this hernia arises from weakness in the testicles, and that matter is spread.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:	And sometimes it comes from a blow to the testicles, and this moisture has many colors:
ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	where it is a color declining to jaundice, or it is without redness, or black, or watery white, and this happens more;
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	and these are the signs to recognize this assembly, for if it is as white as we have said, the abscess is round, and not long, like the shape of an egg, and the testicle is not apparent, because it is surrounded by moisture.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if it has moisture within its own tissue, the abscess is round with a part of the egg, and therefore it is thought to be another egg.
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;	And if the moisture is between the skin of the testicles and the white surface, one feels it well.
donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	Therefore, when you wish to know the color of the moisture, you test throughout the entire cavity, the shape of which is described previously.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to this, therefore, which comes after the cavity, judge of what is within.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors;	And when we treat it with iron, it is necessary that the patient be healed according to his power and the fullness of his body.
puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	Then place him on his back, on something a little high, and put many cloths underneath him;
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions;	Then sit on his left side, and command the minister to sit on the right, and extend the rod to one of the two ribs of the heart of the testicles;
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	Then take a sharp instrument, and cut the skin of the testicles in the middle of their length as far as the point, and let your incision be perfectly straight, dividing the skin of the testicles until white tissue is visible, and carefully scrape it off according to your ability;
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont;	Then pierce the white surface with a large hole, and drain all the water, and then put your hooks, and pull the surface upwards;
et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement;	and do not touch the heart of the testicles, but only the surface;
cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	Cut it entirely or in pieces, even the side subtly, that if you do not cut it wisely, the water will return;
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac;	and if the testicle should pop out during your work, then return it to its place when you have completed the work on the surface;
puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then join the two layers of the heart of the testicles with a suture, then treat it like other wounds, until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc;	And if you find the testicle corrupted by another ailment, you must tie the vessels that are suspensory, fearing the flow of blood;
puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	Then cut the testicle with the entire suspensory ligament, and remove the testicle, and treat it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices;	And if a wound is joined in two parts together, know that these are two branches;
si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	Then cut the other part as you did the first equally, then wipe away the blood, and place wet wool in rose oil on the wound;
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	and put another wool soaked in wine and oil over it, and put it over the two testicles, and put doubled cloths on top of that, and bind it over with all the bandages according to this form:
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil;	Then take two cloths, and fill them with charpie wool according to this resemblance, and let them be joined by stitching at the crotch of the breeches, and one of the ends should be placed over the buttocks down to the back, and the other to the side of the groin;
et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	and the other two ends over the two angles, and let the whole binding be gathered together in the buckle of the breeches;
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	and sometimes this part is treated with cautery instead of an iron cut, and you should take a thin surgical cautery, and cut the skin of the testicles, and heat it as we have said, so that the white surface that contains the water is exposed;
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	Then take the cautery according to this form, and pierce that surface with the prongs, and scorch it with this hot, thin cautery:
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout;	And cut it in every way you can, until you have removed it all;
et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef;	and be careful that the fire does not touch the testicle;
et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve;	and know that this work is more healing;
et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	and be cautious of blood flow, and be aware that the work of cutting is delicate;
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	and if anything opposes you, whether an abscess, or blood flow, or something else, then cure whatever opposes you, according to what has been said before.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit;	And if the patient is fearful, and does not want to undergo this procedure due to its terrifying nature, then administer a perforation, as I tell you, and if you are certain, based on the signs we have discussed, that the watery humor is indeed present, then make the patient sit on a raised seat;
pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors;	then pierce the abscess in the lower part, through the entire breadth, and place the perforation along the length of the body;
et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	and let the opening be wide, so that all the fluid flows out;
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	then place cotton over the area, and bandage it, and let the remaining fluid drain, then treat it until the wound is healed;
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant;	and if the linen bandage does not allow the fluid to exit through the wound opening, then you must insert a reed or the instrument used to draw fluid from hydrops, of which the form is shown previously;
et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	and enlarge the wound's opening, and know that the fluid returns, and gathers after six months or so, and when it has gathered as before, and thus the patient will pass his days.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscesses of the testicles
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	Know that in the treatment of this affliction there is fear in many cases, so I think it's better to leave it alone.
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	and I will tell you the treatment and the characteristics of the abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions;	I say then that many abscesses arise in the body, and especially in the testicles;
et c’est par mout de cas.	and it is in many cases.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	This is to say, by a surplus of sharp and acute humour, spread to the testicles, or by percussion;
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors;	and the color of the abscess is according to the color of the body;
et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	and it does not find any pain, and is a grievous abscess;
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	and perhaps there is a grievous, fearful, and painful abscess, and of a fixed color, and sometimes comes from a broken artery, or from a vein swelling.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it is by a broken artery, it is known by the hot disposition of the abscess when you press it with your fingers;
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	and you should not touch it at all.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	That which is made of vein swelling is known by its disposition to the touch of fingers, and one may well make the incision upon this likeness, and upon the other flesh;
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	and it is that you cut the base of the testicles, then raise the testicle upwards, and pull the white sac away from it, and release the suspensory ligament from all parts of the testicle.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	If the testicle is already stuck to the surrounding tissues, then you must pull and cut the testicle;
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	and if it is exposed on the surface, or within the vessels, you must release all the tension and cut it smoothly.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the tissue’s origin is in the rear, you must cut it all away and extract the testicle, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your work is complete, fill the wound with wool soaked in rose oil and wine, then treat it with other remedies until it is healed.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the testicles
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	This is an abscess enveloped by a covering similar to a boil, with softening of the testicles, and the patient suffers greatly when he moves.
et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	and the treatment for this illness is just as difficult and frightening as the previous one, and yet we will tell you its method, according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment;	You must have the patient sit on a raised seat, then put the supporter for the testicles down to your fingers, encompassing all the vessels close to the penis, and the master shall grasp them and stretch them firmly.
puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples;	Then, cut with a sharp, broad scalpel through the vessels in the middle, until they are exposed, and then cauterize from each side, as we have described in the extraction of the arteries that are in the temples;
puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief;	Then, insert a needle where there is a double thread, and tie it to the first place where the wound occurred, and tie it again to the other end;
puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues;	Then cut them in the middle straight, according to the length of the body, and remove the corrupt moisture;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	Then treat the wound as the others, where pus is generated, so that no vessels spill out to nourish one of the testicles;
car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	For by this, no harm comes, and if pus comes to all the vessels, then the testicles must be removed from all the vessels;
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	So that the testicles do not lose their nourishment due to the incision of the vessels, and dry up and cannot be helped.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rupture of the surface
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The occurrence of this injury is through the incision that comes in the surface, or the extension on the belly in the groin area, so that the intestines descend from that rupture to one of the testicles;
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes:	and this rupture is of the surface, or of its extension, and these two types come from many causes:
ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	or from percussion, or from a jump, or from a fall, or from lifting a heavy load, and by similar things;
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	and the signs when it is from the extension of the surface, are that it happens little by little, over a long time, and does not come suddenly;
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	and the abscesses are equal down to the depths, because the surface presses against the intestines.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs when it is from a cut on the surface, are that it causes sudden pain at the beginning, and the abscess appears differently, under the skin close by, and this is because of the exit of the intestines and the body away from the surface.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the intestines descend with the pouches, and are retained within, and cause great suffering to the patient, especially when they are pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these iron treatments there is fear, therefore they should be avoided.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the method of the treatment is that you instruct the patient to push the intestine back into the wound with their hand, if it can be returned;
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	then let it be held on his neck, between your hands, and raise the thighs;
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	then stretch the body upwards, and cut all the skin of the testicles lengthwise;
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	then put inside the leavres (lips) of the groin, incisions according to your need to open the wound, and let them be such that the pus can exit;
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	then scrape the surface that is under the skin of the testicles, until the hard white surface is exposed on all sides;
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	then put your index finger into what follows the testicle, into what is between the white surface that is beneath the skin of the testicle, and the second surface, and separate what is behind the testicle, and between the second surface;
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	and then pull with your right hand inside the body of the testicles, and stretch the white surface upward with your left hand, and lift the testicle with all its surface towards the groin;
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	and instruct the attendant to extend the testicle upward, and loosen what is above and behind the ligament;
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	and check with your fingers if there is any part of the intestine wrapped around the hard white surface, and if you find anything, put it into the abdomen below;
