Et li signes de celui cui il avient derrier, si est qu’il ne puet espandre son genoil, ne doubler, et est celle jambe plus torte de l’autre, et li angre est mollifié, et est li chiés de la cuixe au leu desoz les costes.	And the signs of that which happens behind are that they cannot extend or bend their knee, and that leg is more twisted than the other, and the groin is softened, and the head of the thigh is in the place below the ribs.
Li ramenemens de ceste semblance de dislocation si est que tu rewarde se li dislocations est anciainne, et elle demore selonc sa disposition, si n’i a nule cure;	The treatment of this type of dislocation is that you must observe if the dislocation is old, and it remains according to its position, then there is no cure;
et n’i covient mie qu’il ait presumption.	and no presumption should be made of it.
Et en celi dont li dislocation est fresche, et c’est des IIII manieres de dislocation, si te haste que tu tornes la jointe, et l’esten dedens et defuer, et la muef a destre et senestre;	And in that whose dislocation is recent, and it is one of the four kinds of dislocation, hasten to turn the joint, and extend it inside and outside, and move it to the right and left;
par aventure si revenra, et n’a mestier d’autre cure.	Perhaps it will return, and no other cure is needed.
Et s’il ne revient en ceste maniere, si covient que tu apareilles I ministre fort, et esten la jambe fort a II mains, ou a I liien que soit liiez sus lou genoil;	And if it does not return in this way, you must prepare a strong assistant, and extend the leg firmly with two hands, or with a bandage tied above the knee;
et uns autres ministres estende sa main desus en teil maniere qu’il boute ses mains desoz ses asseles, puis l’estrigne d’un souef liien sus la cuixe;	and another assistant should extend their hand above in such a way that they put their hands under their armpits, then tighten with a gentle bandage over the thigh;
et uns autres tigne lou chief dou liien;	and another tightens the head of the bandage;
et estendent amont et aval tuit a une fois, tant que li malaide soit levez de terre a une fois, et demoure pendans.	and they pull upward and downward all at once, so that the patient is lifted from the ground at once, and hangs suspended.
Ceste maniere d’estension si est commune as IIII semblances, et se li dislocation est revenue, si com nos avons dit, c’est bien.	This method of extension is common to four similar cases, and if the dislocation is returned, as we have said, that is good.
Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance.	If not, then treatment must be applied to its likeness.
Quant li dislocations est au pardedens, si covient que tu sovines le malaide sus son costeit sain, puis met le liien sus la racine de la cuixe, et le leu qui est desoz l’angre, puis estent le liien en haut devers l’angre, et devers la forcele;	When the dislocation is on the inside, you should turn the patient on their healthy side, then place the bandage on the root of the thigh, and the place beneath the armpit, then extend the bandage upward toward the armpit, and towards the shoulder;
puis preigne uns autres ministres ses bras, et embraice le gros leu de la cuixe malaide, et l’estende au defuer forment:	then take other attendants, and grasp the thick part of the diseased thigh, and extend it strongly outwards:
si revenra a son leu maintenant;	it will return to its place now;
et ceste maniere de dislocation est plus legiere des autres.	and this type of dislocation is less severe than the others.
Et se tu ne la pues serrer en ceste maniere que nos avons dit, si covient que tu lies les II piés dou malaide ensamble d’un fort liien souef sus les II talons, et sus les II genous, et soit li jambe malaide estendue II dois plus que li autres;	And if you cannot secure it in this manner that we have described, you must bind the patient's two feet together with a strong soft bandage over the two heels, and over the two knees, and the diseased leg should be extended two spans more than the other;
puis soit pendus sus le chief d’un fust, et soit en sus de terre II bras de lonc;	then be suspended from the top of a post, and be two arms' length above the ground;
puis comande a I ministre qu’il embraice le chief de la cuixe, et soit uns autres ministres pendans avec le malaide, qui embraice forment la cuixe, car li jointure revient maintenant hastanment.	then command one attendant to grasp the head of the thigh, and let another attendant hang with the patient, grasping the thigh firmly, for the joint will return quickly now.
Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	And when the dislocation is on the outside, the patient lies down, as we have said for those with hip problems, and a bandage is applied tightly to the diseased leg and also to the foot;
puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	then place two embers, one at the head and one at the feet, then place an ember between the patient's thighs in the middle;
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	and have wet cloths placed around it so it does not burn the patient, then each attendant should pull towards themselves, and the one who observes should place the dislocation equally in his hand.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	If it returns, it is good.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	If not, place it on a table, and press it as we said in hip dislocation, and the patient should lie on his sound side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit;	And when the dislocation is in front, it is necessary to extend the ill leg forcefully, and according to what I have said;
et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	and the observer should take pains to be above the ill groin, then press with the other hand, and extend it downwards towards the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches;	And if the dislocation is behind, it is not necessary to extend the ill person downwards, nor to lift him up from the ground, but it is necessary that he be as if the hip were dislocated behind, as we said of the lying down on two hips;
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	and he should lie on his face, and the ligament is extended as we said before, and one must press on the joint against the table;
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz;	and it will be successful when the patient extends his legs, and they are equal;
adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	then join the thighs, and apply the plaster, and bind it with a bandage, so that the hip does not move;
et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus;	and rest for three or four days, then unbind it, and place the plaster over it;
et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors;	and if you see that they are equal, then bind it, as before, and leave it for three days;
puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	then unbind it, and allow it to move gently, until the limb is strengthened.
de la dislocation dou genoil	of the dislocation of the knee
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:	The knee is dislocated in three ways:
c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;	that is to say, inward and outward, and backward;
et ne desalue point devant.	and does not dislocate forward.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	And the sign is that you instruct the patient to bend his leg at the hip, and if it does not fit into his hip, know that it is dislocated;
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	and the restoration of all is that you make the patient sit upright, and extend his leg if he can, and put your back against his face, and place his foot on your feet;
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment;	then take his knee in your palms, and retract between your fingers, then bend the two sides of the knee firmly;
et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	and another attendant extends his foot, so that the knee returns to its place, and the sign is that he fits his leg well into his hip lightly;
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie;	and place the plaster on it, and make the leg fit into the hip, and bind them together firmly for three or four days, then unbind it;
et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	and the patient does not exert himself to walk, until the limb is strengthened.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the limb is not quite right, the attendant should apply strong stretching, as we have said in the treatment of the hip, until it is healed.
de la dislocation dou talon	of the dislocation of the heel.
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heel is sometimes displaced, and sometimes fully dislocated, both inward and outward.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	And the signs are that the ankle is swollen, and extends forward to the part where it is dislocated.
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	The reduction is gentle, and one should gently extend it with their hands when it is only displaced.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	And when it is completely dislocated, you must have the patient sit upright, and two assistants hold firmly on the leg, above the ankle.
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	Then pull the foot towards your right hand, and then to the left hand twice, then extend it upwards, and place the foot firmly upwards.
et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;	And do this twice, as we have said, pushing and pulling the foot.
s’elle revient, c’est bien;	If it returns, it is good.
se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	If not, then restart the procedure, for it will return.
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	And if it cannot return thus, lay the patient on his back on the ground, and firmly place a staff between his thighs, and bind cloths around it so that it does not harm the patient.
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	Then let the assistants hold the thigh, and other assistants extend the foot to their hands or to a tie, which they bind to the top of the foot.
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	Then let each assistant stretch equally, and the staff should be constantly between the patient's thighs to hold the patient while stretching.
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	Then let the surgeon hold the dislocation in his hands, and another assistant hold the healthy leg below, and the dislocation will return quickly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	And when it is in place, put the plaster and bandages on, and bind it tightly, and tie the foot to the leg, and watch the nerves that are above the ankle behind, so that the binding is not too tight.
puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;	Then leave it for two or three days, and if the bandage softens, bind it tighter.
puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	Then unbind it on the third or fourth day, and forbid the patient from walking for four days.
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And if he walks before that time, it is not certain that it will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if boils or sores come there, you must soothe them, as we have said elsewhere, until they are healed.
des dois	of the fingers
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the fingers are dislocated, they should be gently straightened without effort, and this is an easy task.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	And if the dislocation is in any part of the back of the foot, you must have the patient sit on a flat surface, or, say, a table, completely upright, and place your foot on the exposed part of those joints, then press firmly on your foot until it returns to place.
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;	And when it is aligned and nothing is visible, place a table with two supports under the sole of the foot, then hold it firmly, and leave it for three days, then release it.
et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and let it rest until it is healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	of wounds and dislocations together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	When a wound comes with a dislocation, and one wants to restore it, often the patient dies:
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	So be not presumptuous in the cure, if you are not skilled in the art and have not used it long, and if you are not compassionate and merciful and slow, and not hasty.
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	And use at the beginning things to soothe the hot abscess, and leave the patient in God's hands if you see no hope of health;
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	And when you see hope, then reset the limb to its place, before the hot abscess comes there;
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	And when the limb is in place, administer things to soothe the hot abscess, and treat the wound as is proper, with drying ointments;
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	And if with the dislocation there is a fracture, and small bones separated, then set them, and do what we have said in simple maladies;
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	And beware of entering a path of fear, according to what I have said, for this will earn you merit according to your Creator, and for the safety of your arms and body.
